posted:Posted March 8, 2024
msg:The Fuli Westin Hotel is located in the center of Hefei, with a superior location and convenient transportation. I had a pleasant trip here and was impressed by the hotel's services and facilities.

First of all, the hotel's executive lounge breakfast was a pleasant surprise. Every morning, I can enjoy a hearty breakfast here with a variety of fresh food and drinks. The breakfast also offers a wide selection of Chinese and Western dishes, which is dazzling. The ingredients are fresh and delicious, and the breakfast experience is very satisfactory.

In addition, the hotel's rooms are comfortable and spacious with complete facilities. I chose a room on the executive floor, which is exquisitely decorated and fully equipped. The bed is comfortable and the bathroom is clean and tidy. The service of the hotel staff throughout the stay was also excellent, with a friendly attitude, agile and efficient.

In addition, the location of the hotel is very ideal, and there are many famous attractions around it. Famous attractions near the hotel include the ancient city of Hefei, Dashu Mountain, and Luzhou Temple Fair. I only need to walk a few minutes to reach these attractions, which is very convenient. With the recommendation of the hotel staff, I also participated in some local cultural activities and really felt the customs and customs of Hefei.

In general, the Fuli Westin Hotel is a hotel worth recommending. Whether it is the executive lounge breakfast or the nearby attractions, I was deeply impressed. If you have the opportunity to come to Hefei next time, I strongly recommend choosing Fuli Westin Hotel as your place of stay. I believe you will have a pleasant trip.

The hotel is high-end, spacious and bright, the rooms are neat and orderly, and the high floors allow you to enjoy the surrounding scenery. During the spring, if you stay on the executive floor of the hotel, you can watch the fireworks set off around you for free, and the a**osphere is full of the flavor of the New Year. The hotel has strict management, warm and thoughtful service, and standardized polite language. Luca, the front desk receptionist, upgraded the executive twin room for free when checking in, gave a breakfast, and took the initiative to add WeChat to provide services to guests at any time, which was very satisfactory. Opposite the hotel is Bao Gong Temple and Bao Park, and it is also close to Huaihe Road Pedestrian Street and Li Hongzhang Memorial Hall, which is convenient for visiting and playing.
